# MOHAR (https://www.moharbyec.com)

> "Mohar Indian Clothing Boutique is a South Asian dresses and jewelry store located in Herndon, Virginia. We carry a wide variety of lehengas, sarees, blouses, gowns, daily wear kurtis, salwaar, plazzos, and a selection of men's kurtas. We even have special clothing for your little kids! Our bespoke Indian outfits can be customized in all sizes, colors, and styles. We carry readymade bridal outfits for that super special day and also custom make clothing to make your clothing more exquisite and memorable. Bridesmaids, groomsmen, and all other coordinated outfits can be made both in-store and online."
